def ex(cur, table):
    return cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?", (table,)).fetchone() is not None

def count(cur, table):
    if not ex(cur, table):
        return 'missing'
    return cur.execute(f'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {table}').fetchone()[0]

def cols(cur, table):
    if not ex(cur, table):
        return []
    return [r[1] for r in cur.execute(f'PRAGMA table_info({table})').fetchall()]

con = sqlite3.connect('ki_memory.sqlite3')
cur = con.cursor()
print('db: ki_memory.sqlite3')

phase6b_tables = [
    'phase6b_state',
    'phase6b_anchor_pool',
    'phase6b_critic_snapshot',

]

    'phase6a_replay_memory',

    'phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_state',

         'internal_learning_gaps','context_hypotheses',
         'phase5g_experiment_outcomes','phase5h_strategy_outcome_memory',
         'reading_queue','chunk_attention_scores']

        ' ROUND(outcome_score_avg,3), promoted_from, active '
        'FROM phase6b_anchor_pool WHERE active=1 '
        'ORDER BY stability_score DESC LIMIT 10').fetchall())

        ' ROUND(pre_exploration_bias,3), ROUND(post_exploration_bias,3), '
        ' ROUND(pre_inhibition_bias,3), ROUND(post_inhibition_bias,3), '
        ' critic_gate_result '
        'FROM phase6b_plasticity_adjustments ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 8').fetchall())

import sqlite3

def ex(cur, table):
    return cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?", (table,)).fetchone() is not None

def count(cur, table):
    if not ex(cur, table):
        return "missing"
    return cur.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM " + table).fetchone()[0]

con = sqlite3.connect("ki_memory.sqlite3")
cur = con.cursor()
print("db: ki_memory.sqlite3")

phase6c_tables = [
    "phase6c_state",
    "phase6c_meta_control_parameters",
    "phase6c_target_bias_state",
    "phase6c_regulation_events",
]
phase6b_tables = [
    "phase6b_state",
    "phase6b_anchor_pool",
    "phase6b_critic_snapshot",
    "phase6b_effectiveness_events",
    "phase6b_plasticity_adjustments",
    "phase6b_distilled_knowledge",
    "phase6b_l2m_metrics",
]
phase6a_tables = [
    "phase6a_sleep_replay_cycles",
    "phase6a_meta_plasticity_state",
    "phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_state",
    "phase6a_plasticity_adjustments",
]

print("--- counts phase6c ---")
for t in phase6c_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
print("--- counts phase6b ---")
for t in phase6b_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
print("--- counts phase6a ---")
for t in phase6a_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))

if ex(cur, "phase6c_state"):
    print("phase6c_state:", cur.execute(
        "SELECT key,value FROM phase6c_state ORDER BY key"
    ).fetchall())

if ex(cur, "phase6c_meta_control_parameters"):
    print("meta_control_parameters:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT parameter_key, ROUND(current_value,4), ROUND(default_value,4), "
        " ROUND(min_value,4), ROUND(max_value,4), driver_botenstoff, driver_metric, "
        " updated_at FROM phase6c_meta_control_parameters "
        "ORDER BY parameter_key"
    ).fetchall():
        print("  ", row)

if ex(cur, "phase6c_target_bias_state"):
    print("target_bias_state:", cur.execute(
        "SELECT key, ROUND(CAST(value AS REAL),4) FROM phase6c_target_bias_state ORDER BY key"
    ).fetchall())

if ex(cur, "phase6c_regulation_events"):
    print("regulation_events_recent:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT cycle_index, parameter_key, ROUND(pre_value,4), ROUND(post_value,4), "
        " ROUND(delta,4), driver_botenstoff, driver_metric, ROUND(driver_value,4), reason "
        "FROM phase6c_regulation_events ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10"
    ).fetchall():
        print("  ", row)

if ex(cur, "phase6b_plasticity_adjustments"):
    print("latest_phase6b_adjustment:", cur.execute(
        "SELECT cycle_index, adjustment_type, ROUND(pre_plasticity_level,3), "
        " ROUND(post_plasticity_level,3), ROUND(pre_exploration_bias,3), "
        " ROUND(post_exploration_bias,3), critic_gate_result "
        "FROM phase6b_plasticity_adjustments ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 1"
    ).fetchone())

print("safety_facts_rel_questions:", {t: count(cur, t) for t in ["facts","relations","questions"]})

con.close()

===== FILE: tools\show_phase7a_adenosine_homeostat_status.py =====
import sqlite3

def ex(cur, table):
    return cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?", (table,)).fetchone() is not None

def count(cur, table):
    if not ex(cur, table):
        return "missing"
    return cur.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM " + table).fetchone()[0]

con = sqlite3.connect("ki_memory.sqlite3")
cur = con.cursor()
print("db: ki_memory.sqlite3")

phase7a_tables = [
    "phase7a_state",
    "phase7a_adenosine_state",
    "phase7a_adenosine_events",
    "phase7a_sleep_pressure_history",
]
phase6d_tables = [
    "phase6d_state",
    "phase6d_meta_metaplasticity_state",
    "phase6d_saturation_events",
    "phase6d_bias_reset_events",
]
phase6c_tables = [
    "phase6c_state",
    "phase6c_meta_control_parameters",
    "phase6c_target_bias_state",
    "phase6c_regulation_events",
]
phase6b_tables = [
    "phase6b_effectiveness_events",
    "phase6b_plasticity_adjustments",
    "phase6b_l2m_metrics",
    "phase6b_critic_snapshot",
    "phase6b_anchor_pool",
    "phase6b_distilled_knowledge",
]
phase6a_tables = [
    "phase6a_sleep_replay_cycles",
    "phase6a_meta_plasticity_state",
    "phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_state",
    "phase6a_plasticity_adjustments",
]

print("--- counts phase7a ---")
for t in phase7a_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
print("--- counts phase6d ---")
for t in phase6d_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
print("--- counts phase6c ---")
for t in phase6c_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
print("--- counts phase6b ---")
for t in phase6b_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
print("--- counts phase6a ---")
for t in phase6a_tables:
    print(t, count(cur, t))

if ex(cur, "phase7a_state"):
    print("phase7a_state:", cur.execute(
        "SELECT key,value FROM phase7a_state ORDER BY key"
    ).fetchall())

if ex(cur, "phase7a_adenosine_state"):
    print("adenosine_state:", cur.execute(
        "SELECT key, ROUND(CAST(value AS REAL),4) FROM phase7a_adenosine_state ORDER BY key"
    ).fetchall())

if ex(cur, "phase7a_adenosine_events"):
    print("adenosine_events_recent:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT cycle_index, event_type, ROUND(adenosine_level,4), "
        " ROUND(sleep_pressure,4), ROUND(downscale_factor,4), "
        " action_taken, targets_affected, reason "
        "FROM phase7a_adenosine_events ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10"
    ).fetchall():
        print(" ", tuple(row))

if ex(cur, "phase7a_sleep_pressure_history"):
    print("sleep_pressure_history_recent:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT cycle_index, ROUND(adenosine_level,4), "
        " ROUND(wake_activity_since,4), "
        " ROUND(downscale_applied,4), ROUND(effectiveness_before,4), "
        " ROUND(effectiveness_after,4), ROUND(recovery_delta,4) "
        "FROM phase7a_sleep_pressure_history ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10"
    ).fetchall():
        print(" ", tuple(row))

if ex(cur, "phase6a_meta_plasticity_state"):
    print("current_phase6a_bias:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT key, value FROM phase6a_meta_plasticity_state "
        "WHERE key IN ('last_plasticity_level','last_exploration_bias','last_consolidation_bias','last_inhibition_bias','last_revision_bias') "
        "ORDER BY key"
    ).fetchall():
        print(" ", row)

print("safety_facts_rel_questions:", {t: count(cur, t) for t in ["facts","relations","questions"]})

print()
print("NOTE: Adenosine accumulates with 'wake' cycles and naturally forces a sleep-driven")
print("downscaling once its threshold is reached. It is the biological answer to the")
print("saturation problem that phase6d fixes algorithmically.")

con.close()

===== END FILE: tools\show_phase7a_adenosine_homeostat_status.py =====

===== FILE: tools\show_phase7b_endocannabinoid_retrograde_gain_control_status.py =====
import sqlite3

def ex(cur, table):
    return cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?", (table,)).fetchone() is not None

def count(cur, table):
    if not ex(cur, table): return "missing"
    return cur.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM " + table).fetchone()[0]

con = sqlite3.connect("ki_memory.sqlite3")
cur = con.cursor()
print("db: ki_memory.sqlite3")

for t in ["phase7b_state","phase7b_endocannabinoid_state","phase7b_retrograde_signals",
          "phase7b_gain_control_events","phase7b_adenosine_override_events"]:
    print(t, count(cur, t))

if ex(cur, "phase7b_endocannabinoid_state"):
    print("endocannabinoid_state:")
    for r in cur.execute("SELECT key, ROUND(CAST(value AS REAL),4) FROM phase7b_endocannabinoid_state ORDER BY key").fetchall():
        print(" ", r)

if ex(cur, "phase7b_adenosine_override_events"):
    print("adenosine_override_events_recent:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT cycle_index, ROUND(adenosine_level,3), targets_restored, ROUND(dampening_factor,3), reason "
        "FROM phase7b_adenosine_override_events ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10").fetchall():
        print(" ", tuple(row))

if ex(cur, "phase7b_retrograde_signals"):
    print("retrograde_signals_recent:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT cycle_index, signal_type, source, ROUND(magnitude,4), target_key, ROUND(pre_value,4), ROUND(post_value,4) "
        "FROM phase7b_retrograde_signals ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10").fetchall():
        print(" ", tuple(row))

if ex(cur, "phase6a_meta_plasticity_state"):
    print("current_phase6a_bias:")
    for row in cur.execute(
        "SELECT key, value FROM phase6a_meta_plasticity_state "
        "WHERE key IN ('last_plasticity_level','last_exploration_bias','last_consolidation_bias','last_inhibition_bias','last_revision_bias') "
        "ORDER BY key").fetchall():
        print(" ", row)

print("safety:", {t: count(cur, t) for t in ["facts","relations","questions"]})
con.close()

===== END FILE: tools\show_phase7b_endocannabinoid_retrograde_gain_control_status.py =====

===== FILE: tools\show_phase7c_adaptive_boundaries_status.py =====
import sqlite3
def ex(cur, t):
    return cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name=?", (t,)).fetchone() is not None
def count(cur, t):
    if not ex(cur, t): return "missing"
    return cur.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM " + t).fetchone()[0]
con = sqlite3.connect("ki_memory.sqlite3"); cur = con.cursor()
print("db: ki_memory.sqlite3")
for t in ["phase7c_state","phase7c_boundary_state","phase7c_parameter_streaks","phase7c_boundary_events","phase7c_ei_balance_events"]:
    print(t, count(cur, t))
if ex(cur, "phase7c_boundary_state"):
    print("boundary_state:", cur.execute("SELECT key,ROUND(CAST(value AS REAL),4) FROM phase7c_boundary_state ORDER BY key").fetchall())
if ex(cur, "phase7c_boundary_events"):
    print("boundary_events_recent:")
    for r in cur.execute("SELECT cycle_index,parameter_key,boundary,ROUND(pre_min,4),ROUND(post_min,4),ROUND(pre_max,4),ROUND(post_max,4),driver_botenstoff,reason FROM phase7c_boundary_events ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10").fetchall():
        print("  ", tuple(r))
if ex(cur, "phase7c_ei_balance_events"):
    print("ei_balance_recent:")
    for r in cur.execute("SELECT cycle_index,ROUND(glu_pre,3),ROUND(glu_post,3),ROUND(gaba_pre,3),ROUND(gaba_post,3),ROUND(gamma,3),ROUND(alpha,3) FROM phase7c_ei_balance_events ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT 10").fetchall():
        print("  cyc", r[0], "glu", r[1], "->", r[2], " gaba", r[3], "->", r[4], " gamma", r[5], "alpha", r[6])
if ex(cur, "phase6c_meta_control_parameters"):
    print("meta_params (min/current/max):")
    for r in cur.execute("SELECT parameter_key,ROUND(min_value,4),ROUND(current_value,4),ROUND(max_value,4) FROM phase6c_meta_control_parameters ORDER BY parameter_key").fetchall():
        print("  ", r[0], ":", r[1], "|", r[2], "|", r[3])
if ex(cur, "phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_state"):
    g = cur.execute("SELECT value FROM phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_state WHERE key='glutamate'").fetchone()
    gb = cur.execute("SELECT value FROM phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_state WHERE key='gaba'").fetchone()
    print("current glutamate:", g[0] if g else None, " gaba:", gb[0] if gb else None)
print("safety:", {t: count(cur, t) for t in ["facts","relations","questions"]})
con.close()

===== END FILE: tools\show_phase7c_adaptive_boundaries_status.py =====

===== FILE: tools\show_phase7d_slow_wave_status.py =====
import sys, sqlite3
from pathlib import Path
_R=Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
if str(_R) not in sys.path: sys.path.insert(0,str(_R))
con=sqlite3.connect(str(_R/"ki_memory.sqlite3"))
def q(s):
    try: return con.execute(s).fetchone()
    except Exception as e: return ("ERR",str(e))
print("=== PHASE 7d Slow-Wave Status ===")
for k in ("cycle_count","total_slow_wave_sleeps","total_reinforced","total_weakened","phase_version"):
    r=con.execute("SELECT value FROM phase7d_slow_wave_params WHERE key=? UNION ALL SELECT value FROM phase7d_state WHERE key=?",(k,k)).fetchone()
    print(f"  {k}: {r[0] if r else None}")
print("  cycles logged:", q("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM phase7d_slow_wave_cycles")[0])
print("  up_state_events:", q("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM phase7d_up_state_events")[0])
print("  survivors:", q("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM phase7d_consolidation_survivors")[0])
print("  SAFETY facts/relations/questions:", q("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM facts")[0], q("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM relations")[0], q("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM questions")[0])
con.close()

===== END FILE: tools\show_phase7d_slow_wave_status.py =====

===== FILE: tools\show_quality_status.py =====
import sqlite3
con = sqlite3.connect('ki_memory.sqlite3')
cur = con.cursor()
print('STATUS:', cur.execute("SELECT status, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations GROUP BY status").fetchall())
print('CONSOLIDATED:', cur.execute("SELECT reject_reason, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations WHERE reject_reason LIKE 'consolidated_%' GROUP BY reject_reason ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 20").fetchall())
print('HEADING_CLAUSE:', cur.execute("SELECT reject_reason, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations WHERE reject_reason LIKE 'heading_%' OR reject_reason LIKE 'clause_%' GROUP BY reject_reason ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 20").fetchall())
print('PREDICATE:', cur.execute("SELECT reject_reason, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations WHERE reject_reason LIKE 'predicate_%' GROUP BY reject_reason ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 20").fetchall())
print('ACCEPTANCE:', cur.execute("SELECT reject_reason, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations WHERE reject_reason LIKE 'acceptance_%' GROUP BY reject_reason ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 20").fetchall())
print('FACTS:', cur.execute('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM facts').fetchone())
print('RELATIONS:', cur.execute('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM relations').fetchone())
print('QUESTIONS:', cur.execute('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM questions').fetchone())

===== END FILE: tools\show_quality_status.py =====

===== FILE: tools\show_type_refinement_status.py =====
import sqlite3
con = sqlite3.connect('ki_memory.sqlite3')
cur = con.cursor()
print('STATUS:', cur.execute('SELECT status, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations GROUP BY status ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC').fetchall())
print('TYPES:', cur.execute("SELECT candidate_type, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations WHERE candidate_type IS NOT NULL AND length(candidate_type) != 0 GROUP BY candidate_type ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 30").fetchall())
print('TYPE_REASONS:', cur.execute("SELECT type_refinement_reason, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_relations WHERE type_refinement_reason IS NOT NULL AND length(type_refinement_reason) != 0 GROUP BY type_refinement_reason ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 30").fetchall())
print('EVENTS:', cur.execute('SELECT reason, COUNT(*) FROM candidate_type_refinement_events GROUP BY reason ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC LIMIT 30').fetchall() if cur.execute("SELECT name FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='candidate_type_refinement_events'").fetchone() else [])
print('FACTS:', cur.execute('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM facts').fetchone())
print('RELATIONS:', cur.execute('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM relations').fetchone())
print('QUESTIONS:', cur.execute('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM questions').fetchone())

    def read_once(self):
        return {'status': 'old_status', 'promoted_to_facts': 0}

print(install(CorpusReader))

===== FILE: tools\test_v8_phase4_schema_runtime_guard_fixed11.py =====

import sys
from pathlib import Path
ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
sys.path.insert(0, str(ROOT))
import ki_system.v8_phase4_schema_runtime_guard_fixed11 as g
from ki_system.autonomous import AutonomousLoop

===== FILE: tools\test_v8_phase6a_gui_dashboard_restore.py =====

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
from pathlib import Path
import sys
ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
if str(ROOT) not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, str(ROOT))

import py_compile
import sqlite3
from ki_system.gui_phase6a_dashboard_helpers import _latest_phase6a_values, update_phase6a_neuromodulator_dashboard

print("helper_import: True")
py_compile.compile(str(ROOT / "ki_system" / "gui_app.py"), doraise=True)
py_compile.compile(str(ROOT / "ki_system" / "gui_phase6a_dashboard_helpers.py"), doraise=True)
print("compile_gui_app: True")
print("compile_helper: True")

# DB read smoke test
class DummyMem:
    def __init__(self, db):
        self.db = db

class DummyWidget:
    def __init__(self):
        self.text = None
    def configure(self, **kw):
        self.text = kw.get("text", self.text)

class DummyBars:
    def __init__(self):
        self.state = None
    def draw(self, st):
        self.state = st

class DummyApp:
    def __init__(self, db):
        self.mem = DummyMem(db)
        self.neuro_text = DummyWidget()
        self.behavior_text = DummyWidget()
        self.trend_text = DummyWidget()
        self.mood_emoji = DummyWidget()
        self.mood_name = DummyWidget()
        self.neuro_bars = DummyBars()

db_path = ROOT / "ki_memory.sqlite3"
if db_path.exists():
    con = sqlite3.connect(str(db_path))
    app = DummyApp(con)
    ok = update_phase6a_neuromodulator_dashboard(app)
    print("dashboard_update:", bool(ok))
    print("neuro_text:", app.neuro_text.text)
    print("behavior_text:", app.behavior_text.text)
    print("trend_text:", app.trend_text.text)
    print("mood_name:", app.mood_name.text)
    con.close()
else:
    print("dashboard_update: skipped_no_db")

print("facts_rel_questions_check: display_only_no_writes")

===== END FILE: tools\test_v8_phase6a_gui_dashboard_restore.py =====

import pathlib, sys

from ki_system.autonomous import AutonomousLoop
print("cycle_module:", AutonomousLoop.cycle.__module__)
print("cycle_name:", AutonomousLoop.cycle.__name__)
if AutonomousLoop.cycle.__module__ == "ki_system.v8_phase7b1_wake_chain_bridge_release":
    print("OK: cycle points to phase7b1")
else:
    print("WARN: cycle does NOT point to phase7b1")
for f in ["phase7b1_wake_chain_bridge_release","wake_chain_bridge",
          "phase7b_endocannabinoid_retrograde_gain_control_release",
          "phase7a_adenosine_homeostat_release",
          "phase6d_saturation_homeostasis_and_meta_metaplasticity_release",
          "phase6c_bias_persistence_and_self_regulating_meta_release",
          "phase6b_sleep_replay_effectiveness_and_plasticity_adjustment_release",
          "phase6a_neuromodulated_sleep_replay_and_meta_plasticity_release"]:
    print(f + ":", getattr(AutonomousLoop, f, False))
